# 더 월드 40 룩스테라-유적 너머의 비밀 원문 로그

**단단한 허수아비:** 붉은 모루 대장간의 대장장이 그림니르의 의뢰를 마치고 수일 후. 오리진에서 생활하던 여러분은 가벼운 몸을 이끌고 중앙 게시판으로 발걸음 했습니다.

**단단한 허수아비:** 언제나 많은 의뢰들로 가득한 중앙 게시판이지만

**단단한 허수아비:** 유독 눈에 띄는 세가지 의뢰 요청서가 있었습니다.

**GM:** 첫 번째는 에리디안 마탑에서 내려온 의뢰로, 오리진이 보유한 연구자료를 안전하게 호송해 달라는 요청입니다. 의뢰문은 필요 이상의 설명을 피하고 있으며, ‘노출을 최소화해야 한다’는 문장이 반복되어 적잖은 경계심을 남깁니다.

**GM:** 두 번째는 수인족 세 명으로 구성된 모험단이 올린 의뢰입니다. 이들은 유적에서 ‘어마어마한 탐사물’을 확인했다고 주장하지만, 접근을 시도할수록 입구가 닫혀 더 이상 진척이 나지 않는다고 합니다. 함께 들어가, 안쪽으로 진입할 방법을 함께 찾아 보자는 것이 핵심입니다.

**GM:** 세 번째는 오리진의 잡화상이자 물약상인 테오르 마르케인의 의뢰입니다. 모험가들에게 정기 지급하기로 한 물약 공급이 늦어져, 이번에는 직접 제조로 버티기로 했다고 합니다. 다만 그 결정을 실행하려면 대량의 재료 수급이 필요하며, 그 재료를 안정적으로 확보해 달라는 요청이 덧붙어 있습니다.

**GM:** 여러분은 하나 둘 서로를 발견하고는 언제나처럼 동행하기로 하겠군요. (의뢰는 2번으로 고정이지만) 어떤 의뢰를 선택할지 이야기를 해봐야합니다.

**GM:** 여러분은 중앙 게시판에서 만나는 것이다

**메라크 알테메기아:** @턱을 만진 채로 의뢰서들을 보며 뭐가 좋을지 고민하는 중

**매그너스:** @그러면 매그너스가 2번 서류를 떼어 들고 바라봅니다.

**매그너스:** "흠, 수인향우회가 생각나는군"

**메라크 알테메기아:** "어이, 의뢰서 막 뜯지 말라고 새….새?"

**카구야:** @옆에서 보다가 의뢰서를 떼어가는 매그너스를 보며

**매그너스:** @메라크를 보며 말합니다

**메라크 알테메기아:** "씹헐 뭐여 이거"

**매그너스:** "그래"

**매그너스:** "매그너스다"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** (ㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋ

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** (개웃기네

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "자기소개 시간인가?"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "내 이름은 갈기갈기 찢는 이리. 붉은 송곳니 부족 부족장 발자국 없는 범의 두 번째 아들이다."

**카구야:** "어머. 아직 읽고 계신 분들도 있는데 상당히 선택이 빠르시네요."

**GM:** 하늘을 나는 종족 아라코크라… 여야했지만 유독 새로 보이는 매그너스..

**매그너스:** "하? 따라오고싶은건가? 여우?"

**매그너스:** (무려 상위 0.1% 미남이다

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "엄청난 미남이군…"

**메라크 알테메기아:** "뭐야 내가 제일 먼저 왔는데 벌서 사람이 이렇게 는거냐고…는. 다들 누구냐? 다 아는 사이냐?"

**매그너스:** (ㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋ

**메라크 알테메기아:** @다 처음 본다…

**카구야:** "딱히요? 그저 얼마나 그 의뢰에 흥미가 있었는지 궁금해서요."

**매그너스:** (사람은 몰라도 되는데 드루니까 그럴듯하긴해

**매그너스:** "츠하하핫!"

**네모(Nemo):** "오늘은 제가 멧돼지 수인이 되었군요. 네모라고 합니다"

**카구야:** (생각해보니 엘테라만 만났구나

**매그너스:** "뭐, 나도 수인이니까"

**매그너스:** "다른것보다 우선으로 할수도 있지"

**메라크 알테메기아:** "…아니 잠깐"

**매그너스:** "?"

**네모(Nemo):** "예?"

**메라크 알테메기아:** "남자 하나는 머리에 동물 귀가 있고"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "크릉?"

**메라크 알테메기아:** "하나는 멧돼지에, 하나는 새에, 하나는 개라고?"

**메라크 알테메기아:** "뭐냐 이거 브레멘 음악대냐?"

**매그너스:** "츠하하하핫!"

**카구야:** "잠깐만요. 방금 말은 흘려들을 수 없겠는데요?"

**매그너스:** "그럼 내가 닭인건가?"

**네모(Nemo):** "원래는 체인질링입니다. 이거 동물농장이 되었군요"

**카구야:** "누가 개라고요?"

**메라크 알테메기아:** "…개 귀면 개 아니냐?"

**GM:** 브…브레멘 음악대가 뭐지 차원을 넘나드는 지식이 아닌가

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "으하하!"

**메라크 알테메기아:** (일단 동물 음악대라고 하자…

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "그게 뭔진 모르겠지만, 여우! 모욕을 당했군."

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "전사로써 넘어갈 테냐?"

**카구야:** "흑흑. 소녀 슬프네요. 이 모습을 개라고 생각하시다니."

**카구야:** Drizzle 조형계
You conjure up a very light rain, enough to dampen the ground in a 20-foot square but not enough to drink or to put out a fire of any size larger than a candle or match. If sustained for 1 minute, the ground is wet to the touch, and if sustained for 10 minutes, the affected area is slightly muddy or slippery, though not enough to impede movement. In freezing weather, this may generate a coating of thin ice.
Concentration 음 및 동 Action 1분 20ft

**카구야:** @주변에 비내리기

**매그너스:** (널 죽이겠다 선언…!

**메라크 알테메기아:** "?"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** (ㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋ

**메라크 알테메기아:** "여우라고?"

**메라크 알테메기아:** "…쩻든 같은 개과니까 절반은 맞구만"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "그렇다. 꼬리가 굉장히 복실한 게 특징이지."

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "한 번 만져보면…"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "어흐."

**카구야:** "자연스럽게 망측한 소리를 하지 말아주세요!"

**매그너스:** "츠하하하핫!"

**메라크 알테메기아:** "…왜 벌써부터 술이 마시고 싶어지냐 이거…어쩻든"

**Gamemaster:** 전사처럼 보였는데 변태였구나..

**매그너스:** "이것참 진짜 미치광이들의 모임인데"

**매그너스:** "이렇게 된거, 같이 할까?"

**메라크 알테메기아:** @매그너스가 든 의뢰서를 보며 "그래서, 댁들이 동물이니까 수인들 있는 곳으로 가고 싶다 이건가?"

**매그너스:** @손으로 흔듭니다

**네모(Nemo):** "저 빼고 정상인이 단 한명도 없군요"

**매그너스:** "뭐, 일단 나 혼자서라도"

**매그너스:** (?

**매그너스:** (체인질링 엎드려

**메라크 알테메기아:** "멧돼지가 정상이라고 했냐 너는…"

**네모(Nemo):** (ㅌㅌ

**메라크 알테메기아:** "웨어 보어가 수인들 중에서 가장 취급이 안 좋다고, 같은 수인이라고 취급이란게 있어"

**Gamemaster:** 여러분은 함께하기로 하는군요. 의뢰서에는 세명으로 구성된 모험단..이 발신인 이라고 적혀 있습니다.

**카구야:** "어휴… 이런 분들끼리 의뢰를 했다가는 앞날이 걱정되는거에요."

**매그너스:** "츠하핫!"

**메라크 알테메기아:** "일단 난 의뢰를 뭘로 해도 좋겠다만은, 유적이란게 꽤 신경 쓰인단 말이지"

**매그너스:** 카구야의 등을 팡팡 때려주며 말합니다

**매그너스:** "그럼 여우가 같이 가주면 되겠지!"

**카구야:** @회피

**매그너스:** @레클리스

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "유적이라…"

**매그너스:** (카구야 뭐 잘못먹어서

**매그너스:** (체력이 21/23임?

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "그건 전사의 명예를 쌓을 만한 곳인가?"

**카구야:** (마스터가 때렸음

**매그너스:** "나름대로?"

**네모(Nemo):** "자정만 되면 바뀝니다만… 일단은 유적이면 무엇이 있을까요"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** (ㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋ

**GM:** 카구야 heals 2 HP

**헤카트리엘:** "흐아앙… 뭐가 벌써 소란이야아…"

**매그너스:** "유적이라면 무엇보다 적같은거라도 있겠지"

**네모(Nemo):** (그거 아까 제가 파볼로 때린거에요

**메라크 알테메기아:** "보통 유적이란게 뭐겠어. 분명 함정이나 몬스터가 분명히 있"

**매그너스:** "오, 저 아가씨는"

**매그너스:** "분명 날 보며 침을 다셨던 그 아가씨의 동료였나"

**카구야:** @메라크에게 "아 참. 소개가 늦었네요. 전 카구야라고 한답니다. 기억해주시길."

**메라크 알테메기아:** @헤카트를 보자 "야, 방금 내가 동물 가지고 뭐라 해서 미안하다 저기에 동물 같은 요소로 가장 이상한 가시나들이 온다"

**GM:** 룩스테라에서 유적은 매우 흔합니다. 매일 매일 새로운 유적이 발견될 정도죠. 지식을 갈구하고 비밀을 파헤치고 싶은 모험가들의 특성 때문입니다.

**카구야:** (남자 셋인데 가시나들이라니

**노아 레비노스:** "아우."

**메라크 알테메기아:** "…?"@레비를 보면서 의아하다는 표정

**메라크 알테메기아:** "뭐여 이거? 얘가 이렇게 컸던가?"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "변함없이 크군."

**매그너스:** "오, 또 먹힐것같은 느낌이 들어 근질근질한데"

**네모(Nemo):** "오, 수인들이 늘었습니다. 당신만 인간이군요"

**네모(Nemo):** (수인들에게 둘러싸인 메라크

**메라크 알테메기아:** "…야, 이거 나만 종족적으로 왕따 당하는거냐 이거"

**네모(Nemo):** "정 그러면 원하는 모습이라도 있습니까?"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "걱정 마라. 나는 전사라면 대하는 것에 차별을 두지 않는다."

**메라크 알테메기아:** @머리 긁적이며 "아니, 난 인간다운게 좋아서 말이지. 그래도 이번 일 꽤 골때리겠구만…"

**노아 레비노스:** "안녕하세요, 왕따메기아." @소곤소곤

**GM:** 말을 하네

**메라크 알테메기아:** @순간 놀래서 노아에게

**매그너스:** (인간의 말을…!

**메라크 알테메기아:** Unarmed Strike 간이 근거리 무기
Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick, head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a target within 5 feet of you.Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for its effect.Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier. Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger than you and if you have a hand free to grab it. Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger than you.

3 13

11

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** (ㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋㅋ

**매그너스:** (허접www

**노아 레비노스:** "우아."

**메라크 알테메기아:** "이거, 전부터 언어장애 같은건 다 연기였구만 이거!"

**카구야:** "앗! 여성을 때리다니! 그러시면 안돼요!"

**카구야:** @레비노스 쓰담쓰담

**메라크 알테메기아:** "왜 안돼? 맞을만 하면 맞는건 생명의 근본이야"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "저 여자가 말을 못했던가?"

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "여하튼, 그건 중요한 게 아니지."

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "의뢰주에게는 언제 갈 텐가."

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "임시 족장은 누가 맡을 셈이지?"

**메라크 알테메기아:** "이봐. 이러다가 내 이성이 깎이겠다. 슬슬 그 수인들 셋에게 가보자고"

**매그너스:** "츠하하핫!"

**매그너스:** "누가 맡던, 뭐 할일은 변하지 않을테니까"

**네모(Nemo):** Shape-Shifter 특성
As an action, you can shape-shift to change your appearance and your voice. You determine the specifics of the changes, including your coloration, hair length, and sex. You can also adjust your height and weight and can change your size between Medium and Small. You can make yourself appear as a member of another playable species, though none of your game statistics change. You can’t duplicate the appearance of an individual you’ve never seen, and you must adopt a form that has the same basic arrangement of limbs that you have. This trait doesn’t change your clothing and equipment. While shape-shifted with this trait, you have Advantage on Charisma checks. You stay in the new form until you take an action to revert to your true form.

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** Enlarge/Reduce 2레벨 • 변환계
For the duration, the spell enlarges or reduces a creature or an object you can see within range (see the chosen effect below). A targeted object must be neither worn nor carried. If the target is an unwilling creature, it can make a Constitution saving throw. On a successful save, the spell has no effect. Everything that a targeted creature is wearing and carrying changes size with it. Any item it drops returns to normal size at once. A thrown weapon or piece of ammunition returns to normal size immediately after it hits or misses a target. Enlarge. The target’s size increases by one category—from Medium to Large, for example. The target also has Advantage on Strength checks and Strength saving throws. The target’s attacks with its enlarged weapons or Unarmed Strikes deal an extra 1d4 damage on a hit. Reduce. The target’s size decreases by one category—from Medium to Small, for example. The target also has Disadvantage on Strength checks and Strength saving throws. The target’s attacks with its reduced weapons or Unarmed Strikes deal 1d4 less damage on a hit (this can’t reduce the damage below 1).

물질 a pinch of powdered iron Concentration 음, 동 및 물 Action 1분 30ft 1 creatures

**매그너스:** Rage 특성
You can imbue yourself with a primal power called Rage, a force that grants you extraordinary might and resilience. You can enter it as a Bonus Action if you aren’t wearing Heavy armor. You can enter your Rage the number of times shown for your Barbarian level in the Rages column of the Barbarian Features table. You regain one expended use when you finish a Short Rest, and you regain all expended uses when you finish a Long Rest. While active, your Rage follows the rules below. Damage Resistance. You have Resistance to Bludgeoning, Piercing, and Slashing damage. Rage Damage. When you make an attack using Strength—with either a weapon or an Unarmed Strike—and deal damage to the target, you gain a bonus to the damage that increases as you gain levels as a Barbarian, as shown in the Rage Damage column of the Barbarian Features table. Strength Advantage. You have Advantage on Strength checks and Strength saving throws. No Concentration or Spells. You can’t maintain Concentration, and you can’t cast spells. Duration. The Rage lasts until the end of your next turn, and it ends early if you don Heavy armor or have the Incapacitated condition. If your Rage is still active on your next turn, you can extend the Rage for another round by doing one of the following: Make an attack roll against an enemy. Force an enemy to make a saving throw. Take a Bonus Action to extend your Rage. Each time the Rage is extended, it lasts until the end of your next turn. You can maintain a Rage for up to 10 minutes.
Consume Resource Refund Resource
Bonus Action 10분 자신 Self

**매그너스:** Reckless Attack 특성
You can throw aside all concern for defense to attack with increased ferocity. When you make your first attack roll on your turn, you can decide to attack recklessly. Doing so gives you Advantage on attack rolls using Strength until the start of your next turn, but attack rolls against you have Advantage during that time.

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** Hungry Greatsword 군용 근거리 무기 • Graze
A creation of the daelkyr, this weapon is formed from muscle and bone. It may moan, growl, or wail, and it twists in your grip if it doesn’t like you. If any creature attempts to wield this weapon while not attuned to it, it has Disadvantage on attack rolls made using the weapon. Additionally, if you are attuned to this weapon when another creature tries to wield it, the weapon’s hilt extrudes sharp thorns and that creature takes 2 (1d4) 관통 damage each turn. While attuned to and wielding this weapon, you can take a Bonus Action to bond to it, causing tendrils from the hilt of the weapon to burrow into your flesh. You can end the weapon’s bond as a Magic action, causing the tendrils to retract so you can release the weapon. You can remain attuned to the weapon regardless of whether you’re bonded to it. While bonded to it, you gain the following benefits: Secure Grip. The weapon is bound to your hand and can’t be removed from your grasp, voluntarily or involuntarily. If it’s a Two-Handed weapon, only one of your hands is bound to the weapon. Drain Life. When you hit a creature with this weapon, you can choose to expend one Hit Die to deal additional damage with the attack, and as you do, drain the life from your foes. Roll the Hit Die and add your Constitution modifier; the attack deals extra Necrotic damage equal to the result, and you regain an equal number of Hit Points.

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** Hungry Greatsword 군용 근거리 무기 • Graze
A creation of the daelkyr, this weapon is formed from muscle and bone. It may moan, growl, or wail, and it twists in your grip if it doesn’t like you. If any creature attempts to wield this weapon while not attuned to it, it has Disadvantage on attack rolls made using the weapon. Additionally, if you are attuned to this weapon when another creature tries to wield it, the weapon’s hilt extrudes sharp thorns and that creature takes 2 (1d4) 관통 damage each turn. While attuned to and wielding this weapon, you can take a Bonus Action to bond to it, causing tendrils from the hilt of the weapon to burrow into your flesh. You can end the weapon’s bond as a Magic action, causing the tendrils to retract so you can release the weapon. You can remain attuned to the weapon regardless of whether you’re bonded to it. While bonded to it, you gain the following benefits: Secure Grip. The weapon is bound to your hand and can’t be removed from your grasp, voluntarily or involuntarily. If it’s a Two-Handed weapon, only one of your hands is bound to the weapon. Drain Life. When you hit a creature with this weapon, you can choose to expend one Hit Die to deal additional damage with the attack, and as you do, drain the life from your foes. Roll the Hit Die and add your Constitution modifier; the attack deals extra Necrotic damage equal to the result, and you regain an equal number of Hit Points.

You move like the wind. Until the spell ends, your movement doesn’t provoke opportunity attacks. Once before the spell ends, you can give yourself advantage on one weapon attack roll on your turn. That attack deals an extra 1d8 force damage on a hit. Whether you hit or miss, your walking speed increases by 30 feet until the end of that turn.

**카구야:** Bardic Inspiration 특성
You can supernaturally inspire others through words, music, or dance. This inspiration is represented by your Bardic Inspiration die, which is a d6. Using Bardic Inspiration. As a Bonus Action, you can inspire another creature within 60 feet of yourself who can see or hear you. That creature gains one of your Bardic Inspiration dice. A creature can have only one Bardic Inspiration die at a time. Once within the next hour when the creature fails a D20 Test, the creature can roll the Bardic Inspiration die and add the number rolled to the d20, potentially turning the failure into a success. A Bardic Inspiration die is expended when it’s rolled. Number of Uses. You can confer a Bardic Inspiration die a number of times equal to your Charisma modifier (minimum of once), and you regain all expended uses when you finish a Long Rest. At Higher Levels. Your Bardic Inspiration die changes when you reach certain Bard levels, as shown in the Bardic Die column of the Bard Features table. The die becomes a d8 at level 5, a d10 at level 10, and a d12 at level 15.
Consume Resource Refund Resource
Action 1시간 60ft 1 creatures

**카구야:** Inspired Eclipse 특성
When you take a Bonus Action to give a creature a Bardic Inspiration die, you can have the Invisible condition and teleport up to 30 feet to an unoccupied space you can see as part of that Bonus Action. This invisibility lasts until the start of your next turn and ends early immediately after you make an attack roll, deal damage, or cast a spell.
Targets
카구야 카구야
Bonus Action 즉시 30ft Self

**네모(Nemo):** Sorcerous Burst 방출계
You cast sorcerous energy at one creature or object within range. Make a ranged spell attack against the target. On a hit, the target takes 1d8 damage of a type you choose: Acid, Cold, Fire, Lightning, Poison, Psychic, or Thunder. If you roll an 8 on a d8 for this spell, you can roll another d8, and add it to the damage. When you cast this spell, the maximum number of these d8s you can add to the spell’s damage equals your spellcasting ability modifier. Cantrip Upgrade. The damage increases by 1d8 when you reach levels 5 (2d8), 11 (3d8), and 17 (4d8).

You can throw aside all concern for defense to attack with increased ferocity. When you make your first attack roll on your turn, you can decide to attack recklessly. Doing so gives you Advantage on attack rolls using Strength until the start of your next turn, but attack rolls against you have Advantage during that time.

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** Hungry Greatsword 군용 근거리 무기 • Graze
A creation of the daelkyr, this weapon is formed from muscle and bone. It may moan, growl, or wail, and it twists in your grip if it doesn’t like you. If any creature attempts to wield this weapon while not attuned to it, it has Disadvantage on attack rolls made using the weapon. Additionally, if you are attuned to this weapon when another creature tries to wield it, the weapon’s hilt extrudes sharp thorns and that creature takes 2 (1d4) 관통 damage each turn. While attuned to and wielding this weapon, you can take a Bonus Action to bond to it, causing tendrils from the hilt of the weapon to burrow into your flesh. You can end the weapon’s bond as a Magic action, causing the tendrils to retract so you can release the weapon. You can remain attuned to the weapon regardless of whether you’re bonded to it. While bonded to it, you gain the following benefits: Secure Grip. The weapon is bound to your hand and can’t be removed from your grasp, voluntarily or involuntarily. If it’s a Two-Handed weapon, only one of your hands is bound to the weapon. Drain Life. When you hit a creature with this weapon, you can choose to expend one Hit Die to deal additional damage with the attack, and as you do, drain the life from your foes. Roll the Hit Die and add your Constitution modifier; the attack deals extra Necrotic damage equal to the result, and you regain an equal number of Hit Points.

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** Hungry Greatsword 군용 근거리 무기 • Graze
A creation of the daelkyr, this weapon is formed from muscle and bone. It may moan, growl, or wail, and it twists in your grip if it doesn’t like you. If any creature attempts to wield this weapon while not attuned to it, it has Disadvantage on attack rolls made using the weapon. Additionally, if you are attuned to this weapon when another creature tries to wield it, the weapon’s hilt extrudes sharp thorns and that creature takes 2 (1d4) 관통 damage each turn. While attuned to and wielding this weapon, you can take a Bonus Action to bond to it, causing tendrils from the hilt of the weapon to burrow into your flesh. You can end the weapon’s bond as a Magic action, causing the tendrils to retract so you can release the weapon. You can remain attuned to the weapon regardless of whether you’re bonded to it. While bonded to it, you gain the following benefits: Secure Grip. The weapon is bound to your hand and can’t be removed from your grasp, voluntarily or involuntarily. If it’s a Two-Handed weapon, only one of your hands is bound to the weapon. Drain Life. When you hit a creature with this weapon, you can choose to expend one Hit Die to deal additional damage with the attack, and as you do, drain the life from your foes. Roll the Hit Die and add your Constitution modifier; the attack deals extra Necrotic damage equal to the result, and you regain an equal number of Hit Points.

**네모(Nemo):** "억눌린 마력의 파편들이 거친 불티가 되어 흩날리니,
찰나의 순간에 폭발하는 화염의 파동으로 적을 꿰뚫어라."

**네모(Nemo):** Sorcerous Burst 방출계
You cast sorcerous energy at one creature or object within range. Make a ranged spell attack against the target. On a hit, the target takes 1d8 damage of a type you choose: Acid, Cold, Fire, Lightning, Poison, Psychic, or Thunder. If you roll an 8 on a d8 for this spell, you can roll another d8, and add it to the damage. When you cast this spell, the maximum number of these d8s you can add to the spell’s damage equals your spellcasting ability modifier. Cantrip Upgrade. The damage increases by 1d8 when you reach levels 5 (2d8), 11 (3d8), and 17 (4d8).

**네모(Nemo):** Tides of Chaos 특성
You can manipulate chaos itself to give yourself Advantage on one D20 Test before you roll the d20. Once you do so, you must cast a Sorcerer spell with a spell slot or finish a Long Rest before you can use this feature again. If you do cast a Sorcerer spell with a spell slot before you finish a Long Rest, you automatically roll on the Wild Magic Surge table.

You create up to four torch-size lights within range, making them appear as torches, lanterns, or glowing orbs that hover for the duration. Alternatively, you combine the four lights into one glowing Medium form that is vaguely humanlike. Whichever form you choose, each light sheds Dim Light in a 10-foot radius. As a Bonus Action, you can move the lights up to 60 feet to a space within range. A light must be within 20 feet of another light created by this spell, and a light vanishes if it exceeds the spell’s range.
Summon

A near-invisible pulse of arcanomagnetic energy shoots towards a creature within range. Make a ranged spell attack against the target . On a hit, the target takes 1d6 force damage and must succeed on a Strength saving throw or be knocked prone. A creature made of ferrous metal or wearing ferrous armour has disadvantage on this saving throw. This spell’s damage increases by 1d6 when you reach 5th level (2d6), 11th level (3d6), and 17th level (4d6).

An event in your past left an indelible mark on you, infusing you with simmering magic. As a Bonus Action, you can unleash that magic for 1 minute, during which you gain the following benefits: The spell save DC of your Sorcerer spells increases by 1. You have Advantage on the attack rolls of Sorcerer spells you cast. You can use this feature twice, and you regain all expended uses of it when you finish a Long Rest.

**네모(Nemo):** Sorcerous Burst 방출계
You cast sorcerous energy at one creature or object within range. Make a ranged spell attack against the target. On a hit, the target takes 1d8 damage of a type you choose: Acid, Cold, Fire, Lightning, Poison, Psychic, or Thunder. If you roll an 8 on a d8 for this spell, you can roll another d8, and add it to the damage. When you cast this spell, the maximum number of these d8s you can add to the spell’s damage equals your spellcasting ability modifier. Cantrip Upgrade. The damage increases by 1d8 when you reach levels 5 (2d8), 11 (3d8), and 17 (4d8).

The attack uses your spellcasting ability for the attack and damage rolls instead of using Strength or Dexterity. This bow has multiple strings and resembles a lyre or small harp. By strumming the strings while setting an arrow to the bow, you imbue the arrow with magic. You can play one of the following melodies when you use the bow to make a ranged weapon attack. You must choose to do so before you make the attack roll, and you can play only one melody per attack. Melody of Precision. If you’re proficient in Performance, you gain a +1 bonus to the attack roll. If you have expertise in Performance, you gain a +2 bonus instead. Melody of Reverberation. The melody you strum echoes loudly. On a hit, the target takes extra thunder damage equal to your Charisma modifier.

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** Enlarge/Reduce 2레벨 • 변환계
For the duration, the spell enlarges or reduces a creature or an object you can see within range (see the chosen effect below). A targeted object must be neither worn nor carried. If the target is an unwilling creature, it can make a Constitution saving throw. On a successful save, the spell has no effect. Everything that a targeted creature is wearing and carrying changes size with it. Any item it drops returns to normal size at once. A thrown weapon or piece of ammunition returns to normal size immediately after it hits or misses a target. Enlarge. The target’s size increases by one category—from Medium to Large, for example. The target also has Advantage on Strength checks and Strength saving throws. The target’s attacks with its enlarged weapons or Unarmed Strikes deal an extra 1d4 damage on a hit. Reduce. The target’s size decreases by one category—from Medium to Small, for example. The target also has Disadvantage on Strength checks and Strength saving throws. The target’s attacks with its reduced weapons or Unarmed Strikes deal 1d4 less damage on a hit (this can’t reduce the damage below 1).
Consume Resource Refund Resource
물질 a pinch of powdered iron Concentration 음, 동 및 물 Action 1분 30ft 1 creatures

**Cauldron of Plentiful Resources:** This automation requires the following CPR settings to be enabled to function:

This bow has multiple strings and resembles a lyre or small harp. By strumming the strings while setting an arrow to the bow, you imbue the arrow with magic. You can play one of the following melodies when you use the bow to make a ranged weapon attack. You must choose to do so before you make the attack roll, and you can play only one melody per attack. Melody of Precision. If you’re proficient in Performance, you gain a +1 bonus to the attack roll. If you have expertise in Performance, you gain a +2 bonus instead. Melody of Reverberation. The melody you strum echoes loudly. On a hit, the target takes extra thunder damage equal to your Charisma modifier.

**네모(Nemo):** Innate Sorcery 특성
An event in your past left an indelible mark on you, infusing you with simmering magic. As a Bonus Action, you can unleash that magic for 1 minute, during which you gain the following benefits: The spell save DC of your Sorcerer spells increases by 1. You have Advantage on the attack rolls of Sorcerer spells you cast. You can use this feature twice, and you regain all expended uses of it when you finish a Long Rest.
Targets
네모(Nemo) 네모(Nemo)
Bonus Action 1분 자신

**네모(Nemo):** Sorcerous Burst 방출계
You cast sorcerous energy at one creature or object within range. Make a ranged spell attack against the target. On a hit, the target takes 1d8 damage of a type you choose: Acid, Cold, Fire, Lightning, Poison, Psychic, or Thunder. If you roll an 8 on a d8 for this spell, you can roll another d8, and add it to the damage. When you cast this spell, the maximum number of these d8s you can add to the spell’s damage equals your spellcasting ability modifier. Cantrip Upgrade. The damage increases by 1d8 when you reach levels 5 (2d8), 11 (3d8), and 17 (4d8).

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** Hungry Greatsword 군용 근거리 무기 • Graze
A creation of the daelkyr, this weapon is formed from muscle and bone. It may moan, growl, or wail, and it twists in your grip if it doesn’t like you. If any creature attempts to wield this weapon while not attuned to it, it has Disadvantage on attack rolls made using the weapon. Additionally, if you are attuned to this weapon when another creature tries to wield it, the weapon’s hilt extrudes sharp thorns and that creature takes 2 (1d4) 관통 damage each turn. While attuned to and wielding this weapon, you can take a Bonus Action to bond to it, causing tendrils from the hilt of the weapon to burrow into your flesh. You can end the weapon’s bond as a Magic action, causing the tendrils to retract so you can release the weapon. You can remain attuned to the weapon regardless of whether you’re bonded to it. While bonded to it, you gain the following benefits: Secure Grip. The weapon is bound to your hand and can’t be removed from your grasp, voluntarily or involuntarily. If it’s a Two-Handed weapon, only one of your hands is bound to the weapon. Drain Life. When you hit a creature with this weapon, you can choose to expend one Hit Die to deal additional damage with the attack, and as you do, drain the life from your foes. Roll the Hit Die and add your Constitution modifier; the attack deals extra Necrotic damage equal to the result, and you regain an equal number of Hit Points.

**카구야:** 카구야의 턴 Yorumei Rie

**카구야:** Bardic Inspiration 특성
You can supernaturally inspire others through words, music, or dance. This inspiration is represented by your Bardic Inspiration die, which is a d6. Using Bardic Inspiration. As a Bonus Action, you can inspire another creature within 60 feet of yourself who can see or hear you. That creature gains one of your Bardic Inspiration dice. A creature can have only one Bardic Inspiration die at a time. Once within the next hour when the creature fails a D20 Test, the creature can roll the Bardic Inspiration die and add the number rolled to the d20, potentially turning the failure into a success. A Bardic Inspiration die is expended when it’s rolled. Number of Uses. You can confer a Bardic Inspiration die a number of times equal to your Charisma modifier (minimum of once), and you regain all expended uses when you finish a Long Rest. At Higher Levels. Your Bardic Inspiration die changes when you reach certain Bard levels, as shown in the Bardic Die column of the Bard Features table. The die becomes a d8 at level 5, a d10 at level 10, and a d12 at level 15.
Consume Resource Refund Resource
Bonus Action 1시간 60ft 1 creatures

**카구야:** Inspired Eclipse 특성
When you take a Bonus Action to give a creature a Bardic Inspiration die, you can have the Invisible condition and teleport up to 30 feet to an unoccupied space you can see as part of that Bonus Action. This invisibility lasts until the start of your next turn and ends early immediately after you make an attack roll, deal damage, or cast a spell.
Targets
카구야 카구야
Bonus Action 즉시 30ft Self

**카구야:** True Strike 예지계
Guided by a flash of magical insight, you make one attack with the weapon used in the spell’s casting. The attack uses your spellcasting ability for the attack and damage rolls instead of using Strength or Dexterity. If the attack deals damage, it can be Radiant damage or the weapon’s normal damage type (your choice). Cantrip Upgrade. Whether you deal Radiant damage or the weapon’s normal damage type, the attack deals extra Radiant damage when you reach levels 5 (1d6), 11 (2d6), and 17 (3d6).
Action 즉시 자신

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "크아아아아!!!!"

**카구야:** Longbow of Melodies 군용 원거리 무기 • Slow
This bow has multiple strings and resembles a lyre or small harp. By strumming the strings while setting an arrow to the bow, you imbue the arrow with magic. You can play one of the following melodies when you use the bow to make a ranged weapon attack. You must choose to do so before you make the attack roll, and you can play only one melody per attack. Melody of Precision. If you’re proficient in Performance, you gain a +1 bonus to the attack roll. If you have expertise in Performance, you gain a +2 bonus instead. Melody of Reverberation. The melody you strum echoes loudly. On a hit, the target takes extra thunder damage equal to your Charisma modifier.

**네모(Nemo):** Sorcerous Burst 방출계
You cast sorcerous energy at one creature or object within range. Make a ranged spell attack against the target. On a hit, the target takes 1d8 damage of a type you choose: Acid, Cold, Fire, Lightning, Poison, Psychic, or Thunder. If you roll an 8 on a d8 for this spell, you can roll another d8, and add it to the damage. When you cast this spell, the maximum number of these d8s you can add to the spell’s damage equals your spellcasting ability modifier. Cantrip Upgrade. The damage increases by 1d8 when you reach levels 5 (2d8), 11 (3d8), and 17 (4d8).

Cost: 2 Sorcery Points When you cast a spell that has a casting time of an action, you can spend 2 Sorcery Points to change the casting time to a Bonus Action for this casting. You can’t modify a spell in this way if you’ve already cast a level 1+ spell on the current turn, nor can you cast a level 1+ spell on this turn after modifying a spell in this way.

**네모(Nemo):** Earth Tremor 1레벨 • 방출계
You cause a tremor in the ground within range. Each creature other than you in that area must make a Dexterity saving throw. On a failed save, a creature takes 1d6 bludgeoning damage and is knocked prone. If the ground in that area is loose earth or stone, it becomes difficult terrain until cleared, with each 5-foot-diameter portion requiring at least 1 minute to clear by hand. At Higher Levels. When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 2nd level or higher, the damage increases by 1d6 for each slot level above 1st.
DC 15 민첩 내성 굴림 민첩 내성 굴림 Consume Resource Refund Resource
음 및 동 Action 1일 특수 Emanation No Template

**네모(Nemo):** Thunderwave 1레벨 • 방출계
You unleash a wave of thunderous energy. Each creature in a 15-foot Cube originating from you makes a Constitution saving throw. On a failed save, a creature takes 2d8 Thunder damage and is pushed 10 feet away from you. On a successful save, a creature takes half as much damage only. In addition, unsecured objects that are entirely within the Cube are pushed 10 feet away from you, and a thunderous boom is audible within 300 feet. Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. The damage increases by 1d8 for each spell slot level above 1.

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** Hungry Greatsword 군용 근거리 무기 • Graze
A creation of the daelkyr, this weapon is formed from muscle and bone. It may moan, growl, or wail, and it twists in your grip if it doesn’t like you. If any creature attempts to wield this weapon while not attuned to it, it has Disadvantage on attack rolls made using the weapon. Additionally, if you are attuned to this weapon when another creature tries to wield it, the weapon’s hilt extrudes sharp thorns and that creature takes 2 (1d4) 관통 damage each turn. While attuned to and wielding this weapon, you can take a Bonus Action to bond to it, causing tendrils from the hilt of the weapon to burrow into your flesh. You can end the weapon’s bond as a Magic action, causing the tendrils to retract so you can release the weapon. You can remain attuned to the weapon regardless of whether you’re bonded to it. While bonded to it, you gain the following benefits: Secure Grip. The weapon is bound to your hand and can’t be removed from your grasp, voluntarily or involuntarily. If it’s a Two-Handed weapon, only one of your hands is bound to the weapon. Drain Life. When you hit a creature with this weapon, you can choose to expend one Hit Die to deal additional damage with the attack, and as you do, drain the life from your foes. Roll the Hit Die and add your Constitution modifier; the attack deals extra Necrotic damage equal to the result, and you regain an equal number of Hit Points.

If any creature attempts to wield this weapon while not attuned to it, it has Disadvantage on attack rolls made using the weapon. While attuned to and wielding this weapon, you can take a Bonus Action to bond to it, causing tendrils from the hilt of the weapon to burrow into your flesh. You can end the weapon’s bond as a Magic action, causing the tendrils to retract so you can release the weapon. You can remain attuned to the weapon regardless of whether you’re bonded to it. While bonded to it, you gain the following benefits: Secure Grip. The weapon is bound to your hand and can’t be removed from your grasp, voluntarily or involuntarily. If it’s a Two-Handed weapon, only one of your hands is bound to the weapon. Drain Life. When you hit a creature with this weapon, you can choose to expend one Hit Die to deal additional damage with the attack, and as you do, drain the life from your foes. This spell accelerates or decelerates an attack (see the chosen effect below) the instant before it strikes, lessening or multiplying its force. Accelerate. The target takes an extra 2d6 damage from the attack. This extra damage is the same type dealt by the triggering attack. Decelerate. Reduce the damage the target takes by 2d6 (to a minimum of 0 damage). Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. The extra damage or reduction in damage increases by 1d6 for each slot level above 1.

**카구야:** Bardic Inspiration 특성
You can supernaturally inspire others through words, music, or dance. This inspiration is represented by your Bardic Inspiration die, which is a d6. Using Bardic Inspiration. As a Bonus Action, you can inspire another creature within 60 feet of yourself who can see or hear you. That creature gains one of your Bardic Inspiration dice. A creature can have only one Bardic Inspiration die at a time. Once within the next hour when the creature fails a D20 Test, the creature can roll the Bardic Inspiration die and add the number rolled to the d20, potentially turning the failure into a success. A Bardic Inspiration die is expended when it’s rolled. Number of Uses. You can confer a Bardic Inspiration die a number of times equal to your Charisma modifier (minimum of once), and you regain all expended uses when you finish a Long Rest. At Higher Levels. Your Bardic Inspiration die changes when you reach certain Bard levels, as shown in the Bardic Die column of the Bard Features table. The die becomes a d8 at level 5, a d10 at level 10, and a d12 at level 15.
Consume Resource Refund Resource
Bonus Action 1시간 60ft 1 creatures

**카구야:** True Strike 예지계
Guided by a flash of magical insight, you make one attack with the weapon used in the spell’s casting. The attack uses your spellcasting ability for the attack and damage rolls instead of using Strength or Dexterity. If the attack deals damage, it can be Radiant damage or the weapon’s normal damage type (your choice). Cantrip Upgrade. Whether you deal Radiant damage or the weapon’s normal damage type, the attack deals extra Radiant damage when you reach levels 5 (1d6), 11 (2d6), and 17 (3d6).
Action 즉시 자신

**카구야:** Longbow of Melodies 군용 원거리 무기 • Slow
This bow has multiple strings and resembles a lyre or small harp. By strumming the strings while setting an arrow to the bow, you imbue the arrow with magic. You can play one of the following melodies when you use the bow to make a ranged weapon attack. You must choose to do so before you make the attack roll, and you can play only one melody per attack. Melody of Precision. If you’re proficient in Performance, you gain a +1 bonus to the attack roll. If you have expertise in Performance, you gain a +2 bonus instead. Melody of Reverberation. The melody you strum echoes loudly. On a hit, the target takes extra thunder damage equal to your Charisma modifier.

**네모(Nemo):** Sorcerous Burst 방출계
You cast sorcerous energy at one creature or object within range. Make a ranged spell attack against the target. On a hit, the target takes 1d8 damage of a type you choose: Acid, Cold, Fire, Lightning, Poison, Psychic, or Thunder. If you roll an 8 on a d8 for this spell, you can roll another d8, and add it to the damage. When you cast this spell, the maximum number of these d8s you can add to the spell’s damage equals your spellcasting ability modifier. Cantrip Upgrade. The damage increases by 1d8 when you reach levels 5 (2d8), 11 (3d8), and 17 (4d8).

**카구야:** Shielding Word Restriction: Applied before triggering damage - lasts only 1 round
With a word, you coat a creature in a shimmering shield that absorbs the energy of incoming blows. The creature gains 15 temporary hit points the instant before it takes the triggering damage. These hit points last until the start of the creature’s next turn. At Higher Levels. When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 3rd level or higher, you may choose to either increase the range of the spell by 30 feet or increase the number of temporary hit points gained by 5, for each slot level above 2nd.

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** Hungry Greatsword 군용 근거리 무기 • Graze
A creation of the daelkyr, this weapon is formed from muscle and bone. It may moan, growl, or wail, and it twists in your grip if it doesn’t like you. If any creature attempts to wield this weapon while not attuned to it, it has Disadvantage on attack rolls made using the weapon. Additionally, if you are attuned to this weapon when another creature tries to wield it, the weapon’s hilt extrudes sharp thorns and that creature takes 2 (1d4) 관통 damage each turn. While attuned to and wielding this weapon, you can take a Bonus Action to bond to it, causing tendrils from the hilt of the weapon to burrow into your flesh. You can end the weapon’s bond as a Magic action, causing the tendrils to retract so you can release the weapon. You can remain attuned to the weapon regardless of whether you’re bonded to it. While bonded to it, you gain the following benefits: Secure Grip. The weapon is bound to your hand and can’t be removed from your grasp, voluntarily or involuntarily. If it’s a Two-Handed weapon, only one of your hands is bound to the weapon. Drain Life. When you hit a creature with this weapon, you can choose to expend one Hit Die to deal additional damage with the attack, and as you do, drain the life from your foes. Roll the Hit Die and add your Constitution modifier; the attack deals extra Necrotic damage equal to the result, and you regain an equal number of Hit Points.

If any creature attempts to wield this weapon while not attuned to it, it has Disadvantage on attack rolls made using the weapon. Additionally, if you are attuned to this weapon when another creature tries to wield it, the weapon’s hilt extrudes sharp thorns and that creature takes 2 (1d4) 관통 damage each turn. While attuned to and wielding this weapon, you can take a Bonus Action to bond to it, causing tendrils from the hilt of the weapon to burrow into your flesh. You can end the weapon’s bond as a Magic action, causing the tendrils to retract so you can release the weapon. You can remain attuned to the weapon regardless of whether you’re bonded to it. While bonded to it, you gain the following benefits: Secure Grip. The weapon is bound to your hand and can’t be removed from your grasp, voluntarily or involuntarily. If it’s a Two-Handed weapon, only one of your hands is bound to the weapon. Drain Life. When you hit a creature with this weapon, you can choose to expend one Hit Die to deal additional damage with the attack, and as you do, drain the life from your foes. Roll the Hit Die and add your Constitution modifier; the attack deals extra Necrotic damage equal to the result, and you regain an equal number of Hit Points.

**매그너스:** Rage 특성
You can imbue yourself with a primal power called Rage, a force that grants you extraordinary might and resilience. You can enter it as a Bonus Action if you aren’t wearing Heavy armor. You can enter your Rage the number of times shown for your Barbarian level in the Rages column of the Barbarian Features table. You regain one expended use when you finish a Short Rest, and you regain all expended uses when you finish a Long Rest. While active, your Rage follows the rules below. Damage Resistance. You have Resistance to Bludgeoning, Piercing, and Slashing damage. Rage Damage. When you make an attack using Strength—with either a weapon or an Unarmed Strike—and deal damage to the target, you gain a bonus to the damage that increases as you gain levels as a Barbarian, as shown in the Rage Damage column of the Barbarian Features table. Strength Advantage. You have Advantage on Strength checks and Strength saving throws. No Concentration or Spells. You can’t maintain Concentration, and you can’t cast spells. Duration. The Rage lasts until the end of your next turn, and it ends early if you don Heavy armor or have the Incapacitated condition. If your Rage is still active on your next turn, you can extend the Rage for another round by doing one of the following: Make an attack roll against an enemy. Force an enemy to make a saving throw. Take a Bonus Action to extend your Rage. Each time the Rage is extended, it lasts until the end of your next turn. You can maintain a Rage for up to 10 minutes.
Consume Resource Refund Resource
Bonus Action 10분 자신 Self

**카구야:** Bardic Inspiration 특성
You can supernaturally inspire others through words, music, or dance. This inspiration is represented by your Bardic Inspiration die, which is a d6. Using Bardic Inspiration. As a Bonus Action, you can inspire another creature within 60 feet of yourself who can see or hear you. That creature gains one of your Bardic Inspiration dice. A creature can have only one Bardic Inspiration die at a time. Once within the next hour when the creature fails a D20 Test, the creature can roll the Bardic Inspiration die and add the number rolled to the d20, potentially turning the failure into a success. A Bardic Inspiration die is expended when it’s rolled. Number of Uses. You can confer a Bardic Inspiration die a number of times equal to your Charisma modifier (minimum of once), and you regain all expended uses when you finish a Long Rest. At Higher Levels. Your Bardic Inspiration die changes when you reach certain Bard levels, as shown in the Bardic Die column of the Bard Features table. The die becomes a d8 at level 5, a d10 at level 10, and a d12 at level 15.
Consume Resource Refund Resource
Bonus Action 1시간 60ft 1 creatures

**카구야:** Inspired Eclipse 특성
When you take a Bonus Action to give a creature a Bardic Inspiration die, you can have the Invisible condition and teleport up to 30 feet to an unoccupied space you can see as part of that Bonus Action. This invisibility lasts until the start of your next turn and ends early immediately after you make an attack roll, deal damage, or cast a spell.

**네모(Nemo):** Sorcerous Burst 방출계
You cast sorcerous energy at one creature or object within range. Make a ranged spell attack against the target. On a hit, the target takes 1d8 damage of a type you choose: Acid, Cold, Fire, Lightning, Poison, Psychic, or Thunder. If you roll an 8 on a d8 for this spell, you can roll another d8, and add it to the damage. When you cast this spell, the maximum number of these d8s you can add to the spell’s damage equals your spellcasting ability modifier. Cantrip Upgrade. The damage increases by 1d8 when you reach levels 5 (2d8), 11 (3d8), and 17 (4d8).

Dragonmark Feat (Prerequisite: Eberron Campaign, Can’t Have Another Dragonmark Feat) You gain the following benefits. Sentinel’s Intuition. When you make a Wisdom (Insight or Perception) check, you can roll 1d4 and add the number rolled to the ability check. Guardian’s Shield. You always have the Shield spell prepared. You can cast it once without a spell slot, and you regain the ability to cast it in that way when you finish a Long Rest. You can also cast it using any spell slots you have. Intelligence, Wisdom, or Charisma is your spellcasting ability for this spell (choose when you select this feat). Vigilant Guardian. When a creature you can see within 5 feet of you is hit by an attack roll, you can take a Reaction to swap places with that creature, and you are hit by the attack instead. You can use this feature a number of times equal to your Proficiency Bonus and regain all expended uses when you finish a Long Rest. Spells of the Mark. If you have the Spellcasting or Pact Magic class feature, the spells on the Mark of Sentinel Spells table are added to that feature’s spell list. **갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** Hungry Greatsword 군용 근거리 무기 • Graze
A creation of the daelkyr, this weapon is formed from muscle and bone. It may moan, growl, or wail, and it twists in your grip if it doesn’t like you. If any creature attempts to wield this weapon while not attuned to it, it has Disadvantage on attack rolls made using the weapon. Additionally, if you are attuned to this weapon when another creature tries to wield it, the weapon’s hilt extrudes sharp thorns and that creature takes 2 (1d4) 관통 damage each turn. While attuned to and wielding this weapon, you can take a Bonus Action to bond to it, causing tendrils from the hilt of the weapon to burrow into your flesh. You can end the weapon’s bond as a Magic action, causing the tendrils to retract so you can release the weapon. You can remain attuned to the weapon regardless of whether you’re bonded to it. While bonded to it, you gain the following benefits: Secure Grip. The weapon is bound to your hand and can’t be removed from your grasp, voluntarily or involuntarily. If it’s a Two-Handed weapon, only one of your hands is bound to the weapon. Drain Life. When you hit a creature with this weapon, you can choose to expend one Hit Die to deal additional damage with the attack, and as you do, drain the life from your foes. Roll the Hit Die and add your Constitution modifier; the attack deals extra Necrotic damage equal to the result, and you regain an equal number of Hit Points.

Ten berries appear in your hand and are infused with magic for the duration. A creature can take a Bonus Action to eat one berry. Eating a berry restores 1 Hit Point, and the berry provides enough nourishment to sustain a creature for one day. Uneaten berries disappear when the spell ends.

**네모(Nemo):** Catnap 3레벨 • 환혹계
You make a calming gesture, and up to three willing creatures of your choice that you can see within range fall unconscious for the spell’s duration. The spell ends on a target early if it takes damage or someone uses an action to shake or slap it awake. If a target remains unconscious for the full duration, that target gains the benefit of a short rest, and it can’t be affected by this spell again until it finishes a long rest. At Higher Levels. When you cast this spell using a spell slot of 4th level or higher, you can target one additional willing creature for each slot level above 3rd.
Consume Resource Refund Resource

Colossus Slayer Your tenacity can wear down even the most resilient foes. When you hit a creature with a weapon, the weapon deals an extra 1d8 damage to the target if it’s missing any of its Hit Points. You can deal this extra damage only once per turn. Horde Breaker Once on each of your turns when you make an attack with a weapon, you can make another attack with the same weapon against a different creature that is within 5 feet of the original target, that is within the weapon’s range, and that you haven’t attacked this turn.

**매그너스:** Unarmed Strike 간이 근거리 무기
Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick, head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a target within 5 feet of you.Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for its effect.Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier. Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger than you and if you have a hand free to grab it. Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger than you.
Action 즉시 1 creatures 장비 중 숙련

**GM:** 네모(Nemo) takes 3 damage

**매그너스:** Unarmed Strike 간이 근거리 무기
Instead of using a weapon to make a melee attack, you can use a punch, kick, head-butt, or similar forceful blow. In game terms, this is an Unarmed Strike—a melee attack that involves you using your body to damage, grapple, or shove a target within 5 feet of you.Whenever you use your Unarmed Strike, choose one of the following options for its effect.Damage. You make an attack roll against the target. Your bonus to the roll equals your Strength modifier plus your Proficiency Bonus. On a hit, the target takes Bludgeoning damage equal to 1 plus your Strength modifier. Grapple. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it chooses which), or it has the Grappled condition. The DC for the saving throw and any escape attempts equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency Bonus. This grapple is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger than you and if you have a hand free to grab it. Shove. The target must succeed on a Strength or Dexterity saving throw (it chooses which), or you either push it 5 feet away or cause it to have the Prone condition. The DC for the saving throw equals 8 plus your Strength modifier and Proficiency Bonus. This shove is possible only if the target is no more than one size larger than you.

**매그너스:** Rage 특성
You can imbue yourself with a primal power called Rage, a force that grants you extraordinary might and resilience. You can enter it as a Bonus Action if you aren’t wearing Heavy armor. You can enter your Rage the number of times shown for your Barbarian level in the Rages column of the Barbarian Features table. You regain one expended use when you finish a Short Rest, and you regain all expended uses when you finish a Long Rest. While active, your Rage follows the rules below. Damage Resistance. You have Resistance to Bludgeoning, Piercing, and Slashing damage. Rage Damage. When you make an attack using Strength—with either a weapon or an Unarmed Strike—and deal damage to the target, you gain a bonus to the damage that increases as you gain levels as a Barbarian, as shown in the Rage Damage column of the Barbarian Features table. Strength Advantage. You have Advantage on Strength checks and Strength saving throws. No Concentration or Spells. You can’t maintain Concentration, and you can’t cast spells. Duration. The Rage lasts until the end of your next turn, and it ends early if you don Heavy armor or have the Incapacitated condition. If your Rage is still active on your next turn, you can extend the Rage for another round by doing one of the following: Make an attack roll against an enemy. Force an enemy to make a saving throw. Take a Bonus Action to extend your Rage. Each time the Rage is extended, it lasts until the end of your next turn. You can maintain a Rage for up to 10 minutes.

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** Enlarge/Reduce 2레벨 • 변환계
For the duration, the spell enlarges or reduces a creature or an object you can see within range (see the chosen effect below). A targeted object must be neither worn nor carried. If the target is an unwilling creature, it can make a Constitution saving throw. On a successful save, the spell has no effect. Everything that a targeted creature is wearing and carrying changes size with it. Any item it drops returns to normal size at once. A thrown weapon or piece of ammunition returns to normal size immediately after it hits or misses a target. Enlarge. The target’s size increases by one category—from Medium to Large, for example. The target also has Advantage on Strength checks and Strength saving throws. The target’s attacks with its enlarged weapons or Unarmed Strikes deal an extra 1d4 damage on a hit. Reduce. The target’s size decreases by one category—from Medium to Small, for example. The target also has Disadvantage on Strength checks and Strength saving throws. The target’s attacks with its reduced weapons or Unarmed Strikes deal 1d4 less damage on a hit (this can’t reduce the damage below 1).

**헤카트리엘 타이타니아:** Death Ward (Saint Vitruvio's Phylactery) 방호계
You touch a creature and grant it a measure of protection from death. The first time the target would drop to 0 Hit Points before the spell ends, the target instead drops to 1 Hit Point, and the spell ends. If the spell is still in effect when the target is subjected to an effect that would kill it instantly without dealing damage, that effect is negated against the target, and the spell ends.

**네모(Nemo):** Font of Magic 특성
You can tap into the wellspring of magic within yourself. This wellspring is represented by Sorcery Points, which allow you to create a variety of magical effects. You have 2 Sorcery Points, and you gain more as you reach higher levels, as shown in the Sorcery Points column of the Sorcerer Features table. You can’t have more Sorcery Points than the number shown in the table for your level. You regain all expended Sorcery Points when you finish a Long Rest. You can use your Sorcery Points to fuel the options below, along with other features, such as Metamagic, that use those points. Converting Spell Slots to Sorcery Points. You can expend a spell slot to gain a number of Sorcery Points equal to the slot’s level (no action required). Creating Spell Slots. As a Bonus Action, you can transform unexpended Sorcery Points into one spell slot. The Creating Spell Slots table shows the cost of creating a spell slot of a given level, and it lists the minimum Sorcerer level you must be to create a slot. You can create a spell slot no higher than level 5. Any spell slot you create with this feature vanishes when you finish a Long Rest. Creating Spell Slots Spell Slot Level Sorcery Point Cost Min. Sorcerer Level 1 2 2 2 3 3 3 5 5 4 6 7 5 7 9
Conversion Macro

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** Hungry Greatsword 군용 근거리 무기 • Graze
A creation of the daelkyr, this weapon is formed from muscle and bone. It may moan, growl, or wail, and it twists in your grip if it doesn’t like you. If any creature attempts to wield this weapon while not attuned to it, it has Disadvantage on attack rolls made using the weapon. Additionally, if you are attuned to this weapon when another creature tries to wield it, the weapon’s hilt extrudes sharp thorns and that creature takes 2 (1d4) 관통 damage each turn. While attuned to and wielding this weapon, you can take a Bonus Action to bond to it, causing tendrils from the hilt of the weapon to burrow into your flesh. You can end the weapon’s bond as a Magic action, causing the tendrils to retract so you can release the weapon. You can remain attuned to the weapon regardless of whether you’re bonded to it. While bonded to it, you gain the following benefits: Secure Grip. The weapon is bound to your hand and can’t be removed from your grasp, voluntarily or involuntarily. If it’s a Two-Handed weapon, only one of your hands is bound to the weapon. Drain Life. When you hit a creature with this weapon, you can choose to expend one Hit Die to deal additional damage with the attack, and as you do, drain the life from your foes. Roll the Hit Die and add your Constitution modifier; the attack deals extra Necrotic damage equal to the result, and you regain an equal number of Hit Points.

A creation of the daelkyr, this weapon is formed from muscle and bone. It may moan, growl, or wail, and it twists in your grip if it doesn’t like you. **카구야:** True Strike 예지계
Guided by a flash of magical insight, you make one attack with the weapon used in the spell’s casting. The attack uses your spellcasting ability for the attack and damage rolls instead of using Strength or Dexterity. If the attack deals damage, it can be Radiant damage or the weapon’s normal damage type (your choice). Cantrip Upgrade. Whether you deal Radiant damage or the weapon’s normal damage type, the attack deals extra Radiant damage when you reach levels 5 (1d6), 11 (2d6), and 17 (3d6).
Action 즉시 자신

**카구야:** Longbow of Melodies 군용 원거리 무기 • Slow
This bow has multiple strings and resembles a lyre or small harp. By strumming the strings while setting an arrow to the bow, you imbue the arrow with magic. You can play one of the following melodies when you use the bow to make a ranged weapon attack. You must choose to do so before you make the attack roll, and you can play only one melody per attack. Melody of Precision. If you’re proficient in Performance, you gain a +1 bonus to the attack roll. If you have expertise in Performance, you gain a +2 bonus instead. Melody of Reverberation. The melody you strum echoes loudly. On a hit, the target takes extra thunder damage equal to your Charisma modifier.

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** Hungry Greatsword 군용 근거리 무기 • Graze
A creation of the daelkyr, this weapon is formed from muscle and bone. It may moan, growl, or wail, and it twists in your grip if it doesn’t like you. If any creature attempts to wield this weapon while not attuned to it, it has Disadvantage on attack rolls made using the weapon. Additionally, if you are attuned to this weapon when another creature tries to wield it, the weapon’s hilt extrudes sharp thorns and that creature takes 2 (1d4) 관통 damage each turn. While attuned to and wielding this weapon, you can take a Bonus Action to bond to it, causing tendrils from the hilt of the weapon to burrow into your flesh. You can end the weapon’s bond as a Magic action, causing the tendrils to retract so you can release the weapon. You can remain attuned to the weapon regardless of whether you’re bonded to it. While bonded to it, you gain the following benefits: Secure Grip. The weapon is bound to your hand and can’t be removed from your grasp, voluntarily or involuntarily. If it’s a Two-Handed weapon, only one of your hands is bound to the weapon. Drain Life. When you hit a creature with this weapon, you can choose to expend one Hit Die to deal additional damage with the attack, and as you do, drain the life from your foes. Roll the Hit Die and add your Constitution modifier; the attack deals extra Necrotic damage equal to the result, and you regain an equal number of Hit Points.

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** Hungry Greatsword 군용 근거리 무기 • Graze
A creation of the daelkyr, this weapon is formed from muscle and bone. It may moan, growl, or wail, and it twists in your grip if it doesn’t like you. If any creature attempts to wield this weapon while not attuned to it, it has Disadvantage on attack rolls made using the weapon. Additionally, if you are attuned to this weapon when another creature tries to wield it, the weapon’s hilt extrudes sharp thorns and that creature takes 2 (1d4) 관통 damage each turn. While attuned to and wielding this weapon, you can take a Bonus Action to bond to it, causing tendrils from the hilt of the weapon to burrow into your flesh. You can end the weapon’s bond as a Magic action, causing the tendrils to retract so you can release the weapon. You can remain attuned to the weapon regardless of whether you’re bonded to it. While bonded to it, you gain the following benefits: Secure Grip. The weapon is bound to your hand and can’t be removed from your grasp, voluntarily or involuntarily. If it’s a Two-Handed weapon, only one of your hands is bound to the weapon. Drain Life. When you hit a creature with this weapon, you can choose to expend one Hit Die to deal additional damage with the attack, and as you do, drain the life from your foes. **갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** "찢어 발겨라, ｢사메하다｣—!"
조복이 완료된 검은 갈기갈기 찢는 이리의 부름에 응한다. 주어진 명령 아래 순응하며 시동음에 몸을 맡겼다. 검과 몸이 이어진 듯한 감각. 육편의 검이 적의 몸을 수놓는다.

**유적 석조 수호대장:** 캬아아아아 대장 죽는다!

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** Shifting 특성
As a Bonus Action, you can shape-shift to assume a more bestial appearance. This transformation lasts for 1 minute or until you revert to your normal appearance as a Bonus Action. When you shift, you gain Temporary Hit Points equal to 2 times your Proficiency Bonus. You can shift a number of times equal to your Proficiency Bonus, and you regain all expended uses when you finish a Long Rest. Whenever you shift, you gain the benefit of one of the following options (choose when you select this species) Beasthide. You gain 1d6 additional Temporary Hit Points. While shifted, you have a +1 bonus to your Armor Class. Longtooth. When you shift and as a Bonus Action on your other turns while shifted, you can use your elongated fangs to make an Unarmed Strike. If you hit with this Unarmed Strike and deal damage, you can deal Piercing damage equal to 1d6 plus your Strength modifier, instead of the normal damage of an Unarmed Strike. Swiftstride. While you are shifted, your Speed increases by 10 feet. Additionally, you can move up to 10 feet as a Reaction when a creature ends its turn within 5 feet of you. This reactive movement doesn’t provoke Opportunity Attacks. Wildhunt. While shifted, you have Advantage on Wisdom checks. Additionally, no creature within 30 feet of you can have Advantage on an attack roll against you unless you have the Incapacitated condition.

**메라크 알테메기아:** Hunter's Mark 예지계
You magically mark one creature you can see within range as your quarry. Until the spell ends, you deal an extra 1d6 Force damage to the target whenever you hit it with an attack roll. You also have Advantage on any Wisdom (Perception or Survival) check you make to find it. If the target drops to 0 Hit Points before this spell ends, you can take a Bonus Action to move the mark to a new creature you can see within range. Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. Your Concentration can last longer with a spell slot of level 3–4 (up to 8 hours) or 5+ (up to 24 hours).
Concentration 음 Bonus Action 1시간 90ft 1 creatures

**카구야:** True Strike 예지계
Guided by a flash of magical insight, you make one attack with the weapon used in the spell’s casting. The attack uses your spellcasting ability for the attack and damage rolls instead of using Strength or Dexterity. If the attack deals damage, it can be Radiant damage or the weapon’s normal damage type (your choice). Cantrip Upgrade. Whether you deal Radiant damage or the weapon’s normal damage type, the attack deals extra Radiant damage when you reach levels 5 (1d6), 11 (2d6), and 17 (3d6).
Action 즉시 자신

**카구야:** Longbow of Melodies 군용 원거리 무기 • Slow
This bow has multiple strings and resembles a lyre or small harp. By strumming the strings while setting an arrow to the bow, you imbue the arrow with magic. You can play one of the following melodies when you use the bow to make a ranged weapon attack. You must choose to do so before you make the attack roll, and you can play only one melody per attack. Melody of Precision. If you’re proficient in Performance, you gain a +1 bonus to the attack roll. If you have expertise in Performance, you gain a +2 bonus instead. Melody of Reverberation. The melody you strum echoes loudly. On a hit, the target takes extra thunder damage equal to your Charisma modifier.

**네모(Nemo):** Mirror Image 2레벨 • 환영계
Three illusory duplicates of yourself appear in your space. Until the spell ends, the duplicates move with you and mimic your actions, shifting position so it’s impossible to track which image is real. Each time a creature hits you with an attack roll during the spell’s duration, roll a d6 for each of your remaining duplicates. If any of the d6s rolls a 3 or higher, one of the duplicates is hit instead of you, and the duplicate is destroyed. The duplicates otherwise ignore all other damage and effects. The spell ends when all three duplicates are destroyed. A creature is unaffected by this spell if it has the Blinded condition, Blindsight, or Truesight.
Consume Resource Refund Resource
음 및 동 Action 1분 자신 Self

Cost: 2 Sorcery Points When you cast a spell that has a casting time of an action, you can spend 2 Sorcery Points to change the casting time to a Bonus Action for this casting. You can’t modify a spell in this way if you’ve already cast a level 1+ spell on the current turn, nor can you cast a level 1+ spell on this turn after modifying a spell in this way.

**네모(Nemo):** Sorcerous Burst 방출계
You cast sorcerous energy at one creature or object within range. Make a ranged spell attack against the target. On a hit, the target takes 1d8 damage of a type you choose: Acid, Cold, Fire, Lightning, Poison, Psychic, or Thunder. If you roll an 8 on a d8 for this spell, you can roll another d8, and add it to the damage. When you cast this spell, the maximum number of these d8s you can add to the spell’s damage equals your spellcasting ability modifier. Cantrip Upgrade. The damage increases by 1d8 when you reach levels 5 (2d8), 11 (3d8), and 17 (4d8).

**갈기갈기 찢는 이리:** Hungry Greatsword 군용 근거리 무기 • Graze
A creation of the daelkyr, this weapon is formed from muscle and bone. It may moan, growl, or wail, and it twists in your grip if it doesn’t like you. If any creature attempts to wield this weapon while not attuned to it, it has Disadvantage on attack rolls made using the weapon. Additionally, if you are attuned to this weapon when another creature tries to wield it, the weapon’s hilt extrudes sharp thorns and that creature takes 2 (1d4) 관통 damage each turn. While attuned to and wielding this weapon, you can take a Bonus Action to bond to it, causing tendrils from the hilt of the weapon to burrow into your flesh. You can end the weapon’s bond as a Magic action, causing the tendrils to retract so you can release the weapon. You can remain attuned to the weapon regardless of whether you’re bonded to it. While bonded to it, you gain the following benefits: Secure Grip. The weapon is bound to your hand and can’t be removed from your grasp, voluntarily or involuntarily. If it’s a Two-Handed weapon, only one of your hands is bound to the weapon. Drain Life. When you hit a creature with this weapon, you can choose to expend one Hit Die to deal additional damage with the attack, and as you do, drain the life from your foes. Roll the Hit Die and add your Constitution modifier; the attack deals extra Necrotic damage equal to the result, and you regain an equal number of Hit Points.

**메라크 알테메기아:** Hunter's Mark Hunter's Mark: Move
You magically mark one creature you can see within range as your quarry. Until the spell ends, you deal an extra 1d6 Force damage to the target whenever you hit it with an attack roll. You also have Advantage on any Wisdom (Perception or Survival) check you make to find it. If the target drops to 0 Hit Points before this spell ends, you can take a Bonus Action to move the mark to a new creature you can see within range. Using a Higher-Level Spell Slot. Your Concentration can last longer with a spell slot of level 3–4 (up to 8 hours) or 5+ (up to 24 hours).
Concentration 음 Bonus Action 1시간 90ft 1 creatures
